[38;5;252m[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mMesarthim is the third and final stage of the ARIES[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mchallenge. It requires exploiting a x86_[0m[38;5;252m64 protobuf[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mbinary which introduced a small heap BOF using the size[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mchanges between protobuf variable length integers. We[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mcan exploit this vulnerability by adding new entries in[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mthe the existing protobuf structure. This allows us to[38;5;252m [0m[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mdo arbitrary heap allocation, with arbitrary data and[38;5;252m [0m[38;5;252m [0m[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mfinally achieve RCE. Due to being a space challenge the[0m
[0m[38;5;252m[0m  [38;5;252mentire payload must be send at once without interactive[0m
